< text>
My order: Chicken Veggie, More Veggie(which means less rice), and Brown Rice.
Always delicious and always affordable!
I did notice they are hoarding the enjoyable teriyaki sauce now... Which is a shame because I would take about a dozen and save it for later...don't judge me until you've tasted its glory.
But this is the perfect place for a quick bite to eat that's equally filling, cheap and tasty.

Not a lot of outdoor seating and they do share a location with Stans Donuts. Goodluck trying to ignore the amazing aroma of fried dough....yummmm

What more can I say!<//text>

<Pics>None</Pics><text>We have lived at the Legacy for over a year now and really could not have picked a better home. There are so many advantages to this place. First, the staff is great. Everyone is very friendly. The concierges and leasing agents are so helpful and they have done a great job of getting to know us. Second, the location is perfect. We can walk to bars, restaurants, UCLA hospital, hot yoga, regular yoga (there are also 3 gyms within walking distance - Equinox, LA Fitness and Kinross Rec), the grocery store, Target, nail salons, the tailor, the dry cleaners....the list goes on. For people like myself who are not accustomed to LA traffic, having options within walking distance is a big plus. Third, the place is beautiful. The lobby is so pretty and such a nice space to come home to. We love the dark floors of our apartment. We have a 1 bedroom but there is plenty of room for us, our things, and our pets. We don't feel cramped or confined. Fourth, the pool area is a plus. The pool chairs are comfy and the hot tub is perfect after a long hike. There are also grills that are open for use by the residents! Finally, if you don't want to walk to one of the gym's nearby no worries there is one downstairs. It has free weights, a squat rack, treadmills, and an aerobics room. It is never crowded and it is so nice to have a place to get a quick workout it if you need to mix up your environment.
On the downside: 1. totally out of the control of the apartment managers- the traffic on Wilshire Blvd is a bit much sometimes. If you are looking for a quiet outdoor space, rent a unit on the north side, or on one of the higher floors.  2. While you can have guests, pool parties are not allowed which kind of sticks. But is also understandable as people can get out of hand.  3. Tandem parking- really kind of a first-world problem as we are fortunate to have 2 cars, but it is a bit annoying to have to move cars when schedules change.
OVERALL: 10/10 would live here again.</text></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
The amount of red tape Psycare lends its patients isn't worth seeing a doctor in this office. <Text>This is one of my favorites! Privately owned,  not a chain & has been there ever since I was a kid! That's some time now, but we won't give it a number.  They have the best doughnuts in the county & fantastic breakfast choices as well. They make some of the best quiches around with a variety of flavors to choose from.  They also have some bomb breakfast burritos, the bacon is my favorite but the sausage is my husbands favorite.  They also have a couple different breakfast sandwiches to offer as well. There are also a few different coffees to choose from to get you down the road. This is a cozy small town just right feel to it establishment.  The line during busy hours is usually to the door,  so I suggest go before or after.  It's a small parking lot but has a lot of curb side parking which makes it easy.  The service is excellent!< /Text><pictures>None<//pictures><resp>None< /resp><GmapID>0x80ecc357dffd74dd:0xb0049eda2a15f774</GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<Rating>2</Rating>< review>
As a bit of a preamble, I want to make it clear that I have no malicious intent in my review. Everyone who works in the office has been extremely polite, professional, and helpful - they are the sole redeeming quality of Esplanade. That being said, I can only be honest about my experience living here for the last 10 months. And while individual experiences may obviously vary, you should know that moving here means that there is a high probability that you will find yourself in a similar situation as is about to be mentioned.

My wife and I have tried our hardest to feel comfortable here. However, owing to the layout of the complex, we cannot tolerate this place any longer and will be moving next month. The main factors are twofold: noise and parking. Since the units are so close to each other, you will constantly hear your neighbors all around you, many of them screaming and unruly children who run amok day in and day out. (Why their parents allow this is beyond me.) During the spring and summer months especially, many of your neighbors will keep their windows and doors fully open while they have their TVs on at seemingly maximum volume and also have loud conversations late into the night when people who have to wake up early for work try to get some sleep. I lived at BRE Esplanade for five years. The majority of your neighbors will be (very young) recruits at Miramar who can break their lease at any time. It's not uncommon to see a group of loud drunks move in next to you, and have moved out six weeks later.
